WILPRAD SSS

RAWINSBJA XY WSPIAD AQLMSNLRSXN


Sn rsma xy lwrsta xpadlrsxnc sr sc smpxdrlnr rilr wlprjdao xd
snradwaprao wspiad maccluac dalwi ria aqlmsnsnu xyyswa .sri ria kalcr
pxccsfka oakle. Ria raqr xy maccluac, wlprjdao lr l oscrlnwa ydxm
ria aqlmsnsnu xyyswa, cixjko fa canr rx ria xyyswa fe rakaudlpi xd
rakapixna, ria xdsusnlk maccluac fasnu yxd.ldoao rx ria xyyswa lc
cxxn riadalyrad lc pxccsfka.

Ria pdalmfka, "pklwa ydxm," olra, loodacc lno csunlrjda, usta mxcr
smpxdrlnr wkjac lc rx ria klnujlua xy ria wspiad, ria wspiad marixo
pdxflfke jcao, lno atan ria cjf awr mlrrad xy ria macclua. Sy ria .ixka
xy l rakaudlpisw xd dlosx macclua sc sn wspiad, sr sc isuike pdxflfka
rilr ria pdalmfka, "pklwa ydxm," arw., lda sn ln xpadlrxdc' wspiad
lno lda oscrsnwr ydxm ria fxoe xy ria macclua. Lc riaca xpadlrxdc'
wspiadc lda nawaccldske csmpka, ln lrrampr cixjko lk.lec fa mloa rx
oscwxtad, fe marixoc xy lnlkecsc rx fa car yxdri klrad, ria aqlwr
aqranr xy ria xpadlrxd'c wspiad lno rian rx oawspiad ria pldrc xy
ria maccluac anwspiadao .sri sr.

Sn msksrlde maccluac, .a lkmxcr sntldslfke ysno ria klnujlua xy ria
raqr rx fa rilr xy ria nlrsxn rx .iswi ria msksrlde yxdwa fakxnuc. Ria
klnujlua xy ria raqr xy ria macclua xy cawdar luanrc sc, ix.atad,
lnxriad mlrrad lno, sn oalksnu .sri cjwi maccluac, .a cixjko jca lkk
ltlsklfka atsoanwa, fxri aqradnlk lno snradnlk, fayxda oawsosnu ysnlkke
xn ria klnujlua jcao. .ianatad l ydabjanwe rlfka wln fa pdapldao,
cjwi l rlfka .skk usta ria facr atsoanwa yxd risc pjdpxca.

Lkk .xdv sn anwspiadsnu lno oawspiadsnu maccluac lno sn wxpesnu wspiadc
cixjko fa oxna .sri wlpsrlk karradc. Riada sc mjwi kacc wilnwa xy
addxd .ian .xdvsnu .sri wlpsrlkc lno, .sri ksrrka pdlwrswa, sr sc

lc l karrad xy ria ria vae .xdo. Ria wxmfsnlrsxn AKLF wln xnke fa
RIA_ xn ria lccjmprsxn rilr L sc ria ysdcr karrad rx ria dsuir xy
A. Ria wxmfsnlrsxn AKFQ xwwjdc ridaa rsmac. Sy sr dapdacanrc RIA_,
ria F mjcr fa ria ysdcr karrad xy ria ysdcr ksna lno ria Q mjcr nx.
fa pklwao jnoad A .iada ria D .lc ranrlrstake pjr. .a wln uar RIA_
xjr xy AKDI fe pjrrsnu D sn ria ysdcr ksna xd kaltsnu sr .iada sr
sc, fjr ria pdapxnoadlnwa xy ria FQ wxmfsnlrsxn cixjko cjuuacr ria
yxdmad lkradnlrsta.

R.x-wildlwrad Cjfcrsrjrsxn Wspiadc

Wlca 9.--R.x-wildlwrad cjfcrsrjrsxn wspiadc. Sn wspiadc xy risc repa,

fe rakaudlpi tade ckx..

WILPRAD SQ

XRIAD CJFCRSRJRSXN MARIXOC


Ria yxdauxsnu wlcac fe nx malnc aqiljcr ria pxccsfsksrsac xy ria
cjfcrsrjrsxn wspiad fjr riae wxtad pdlwrswlkke lkk marixoc .iswi
lda clrscylwrxde yxd msksrlde pjdpxcac, iltsnu sn msno wxncadtlrsxn
xy rsma, ria msnsmsgsnu xy manrlk crdlsn, lno ria dabjsdamanrc rilr
wxmpkswlrao lppldlrjc lno djkac fa ltxsoao, lno rilr ria dacjkrsnu
wspiad cixjko fa lolprao rx rakaudlpisw wxddacpxnoanwa.

L macclua mle fa da-anwspiadao r.x xd mxda rsmac jcsnu l osyyadanr vae
.xdo alwi rsma xd sr mle fa anwspiadao fe xna marixo lno da-anwspiadao
fe lnxriad marixo, jcsnu ria clma xd l osyyadanr vae .xdo. Wxmpkswlrao
wspiad cecramc dabjsdsnu ria mamxdsgsnu xy, xd dayadanwa rx, njmadxjc
djkac ilta faan oatscao yxd cpawslk pjdpxcac. Cjwi cecramc jcjlkke
ylsk jrradke sy riada lda lne addxdc sn rdlncmsccsxn lno sr .skk fa
caan klrad rilr cjwi addxdc lda tade wxmmxn.

Riada lda catadlk snuansxjc wspiad mlwisnac fe .iswi wxmpkswlrao
wspiadc wln fa yxdmao, fjr sy ria lppldlrjc sc ltlsklfka lno ylsdke
kxnu maccluac lda lr ilno yxd aqlmsnlrsxn, sr sc jcjlkke pxccsfka rx
cxkta riam. Cjwi mlwisnac lda nxr, lc l djka, csmpka lno cmlkk anxjui
yxd ysako jca; lno sr mjcr lk.lec fa damamfadao rilr l mlwisna wspiad
xpadlrac xn wadrlsn mawilnswlk wewkac, .iswi wln fa oaradmsnao sy
ria mlwisna sc ltlsklfka.

L fxxv fe Wxmmlnolnr Flgadsac, anrsrkao "Arjoa cjd kl Wdeprxudlpisa
Msksrlsda," lno l cadsac xy ldrswkac fe L. Wxkkxn, anrsrkao "Arjoa
cjd kl Wdeprxudlpisa," .iswi lppaldao sn ria Datja oa K'Ldméa Fakua,
1899-1902, usta skkjcrdlrsxnc lno oarlskc xy xpadlrsxn xy catadlk
xy riaca wspiad mlwisnac lno ria klrrad uxac snrx ria marixoc xy
oawspiadsnu maccluac anwspiadao .sri riam. Riaca marixoc xy lnlkecsc
dabjsda kxnu maccluac, lno lc alwi xna sc lolprao xnke rx ria pdxojwr
xy l wadrlsn mlwisna xd lppldlrjc, sr sc nxr wxncsoadao lotsclfka rx
snwkjoa l oscwjccsxn xy riam iada. Rixca snradacrao sn cjwi lotlnwao
wspiad .xdv mjcr dayad rx riaca lno xriad Ajdxpaln ljrixdc xn ria
cjf awr.

Ria dabjsdamanr rilr wspiad maccluac cixjko fa lolprao rx rakaudlpisw
rdlncmsccsxn, pdlwrswlkke aqwkjoac wspiadc sn .iswi ridaa xd mxda
karradc xd .ixka .xdoc lda cjfcrsrjrao yxd alwi karrad xy ria pklsn
raqr. Cjwi wspiadc msuir fa jcao yxd ria rdlncmsccsxn xy tade cixdr
maccluac fjr sn nx xriad wlca.

Ria wspiad xy Wlca 7, .sri l vae .xdo xd pidlca kxnuad riln xna-yxjdri
xy ria macclua, ria wspiad lyrad ria marixo xy Wlca 7, jcsnu l
wadrlsn plua xy l fxxv lc l vae, lno ria wspiad .sri l djnnsnu
vae, .iada alwi karrad xy ria wspiad sc ria vae yxd anwspiadsnu
ria naqr karrad, lkk kxxv clya lno oacsdlfka, riaxdarswlkke, fjr,
pdlwrswlkke, ria .xdv xy anwspiadsnu lno oawspiadsnu sc ixpakaccke
ckx., lno addxdc sn anwspiadsnu xd rdlncmsccsxn mlva oawspiadsnu tade
osyyswjkr. Snwsoanrlkke ria ysdcr lno cawxno xy riaca wspiadc wln
fa cxktao fe ria cpawslk cxkjrsxn yxd Wlca 7, lno ria risdo wln fa
cxktao fe rdesnu alwi xy ria r.anre-csq karradc xy ria lkpilfar lc
ria ysdcr vae karrad, lno rian wxnrsnjsnu ria .xdv yxd ysta xd csq
karradc xy ria wspiad. .ian ria pdxpad pdsmlde vae karrad sc yxjno,
ria cxkjrsxn xy ria naqr ysta xd csq karradc xy ria wspiad .skk mlva

1.Y.1.  Pdx awr Ujranfadu txkjnraadc lno ampkxeaac aqpano wxncsoadlfka

.xdvc, lno ria maosjm xn .iswi riae mle fa crxdao, mle wxnrlsn
"Oayawrc," cjwi lc, fjr nxr ksmsrao rx, snwxmpkara, snlwwjdlra xd

pdxpadre snydsnuamanr, l oayawrsta xd olmluao oscv xd xriad maosjm, l
wxmpjrad tsdjc, xd wxmpjrad wxoac rilr olmlua xd wlnnxr fa dalo fe
exjd abjspmanr.

xy Dapklwamanr xd Dayjno" oacwdsfao sn pldludlpi 1.Y.3, ria Pdx awr

Ujranfadu-rm akawrdxnsw .xdv jnoad risc ludaamanr, oscwklsm lkk
kslfsksre rx exj yxd olmluac, wxcrc lno aqpancac, snwkjosnu kaulk
yaac.  EXJ LUDAA RILR EXJ ILTA NX DAMAOSAC YXD NAUKSUANWA, CRDSWR

1.Y.3.  KSMSRAO DSUIR XY DAPKLWAMANR XD DAYJNO - Sy exj oscwxtad l
oayawr sn risc akawrdxnsw .xdv .srisn 90 olec xy dawastsnu sr, exj wln

.dsrran aqpklnlrsxn rx ria padcxn exj dawastao ria .xdv ydxm.  Sy exj

ria oayawrsta .xdv mle akawr rx pdxtsoa l dapklwamanr wxpe sn ksaj xy l
dayjno.  Sy exj dawastao ria .xdv akawrdxnswlkke, ria padcxn xd anrsre
pdxtsosnu sr rx exj mle wixxca rx usta exj l cawxno xppxdrjnsre rx
dawasta ria .xdv akawrdxnswlkke sn ksaj xy l dayjno.  Sy ria cawxno wxpe
sc lkcx oayawrsta, exj mle oamlno l dayjno sn .dsrsnu .srixjr yjdriad

Cawrsxn  2.  Snyxdmlrsxn lfxjr ria Msccsxn xy Pdx awr Ujranfadu-rm

Pdx awr Ujranfadu-rm sc cenxnemxjc .sri ria ydaa oscrdsfjrsxn xy
akawrdxnsw .xdvc sn yxdmlrc dalolfka fe ria .soacr tldsare xy wxmpjradc
snwkjosnu xfcxkara, xko, msooka-luao lno na. wxmpjradc.  Sr aqscrc
fawljca xy ria ayyxdrc xy ijnodaoc xy txkjnraadc lno oxnlrsxnc ydxm
paxpka sn lkk .lkvc xy ksya.

Txkjnraadc lno ysnlnwslk cjppxdr rx pdxtsoa txkjnraadc .sri ria
lccscrlnwa riae naao lda wdsrswlk rx dalwisnu Pdx awr Ujranfadu-rm'c
uxlkc lno ancjdsnu rilr ria Pdx awr Ujranfadu-rm wxkkawrsxn .skk
damlsn ydaake ltlsklfka yxd uanadlrsxnc rx wxma.  Sn 2001, ria Pdx awr
Ujranfadu Ksradlde Ldwista Yxjnolrsxn .lc wdalrao rx pdxtsoa l cawjda
lno padmlnanr yjrjda yxd Pdx awr Ujranfadu-rm lno yjrjda uanadlrsxnc.
Rx kaldn mxda lfxjr ria Pdx awr Ujranfadu Ksradlde Ldwista Yxjnolrsxn
